Entry: 2.
Entry: 4
Entry:            If during any quarter, 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: desires to increase its overall requirements for any Product in excess of 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  percent (
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry: %) of its total requirement for such Product during any of three immediately preceding quarters, 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall be given, if needed, 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  months lead time for the acquisition of new or additional tooling, as the case may be, to satisfy the increased demand.  
Entry: Seller
Entry:  may charge 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: for the cost and expenses of such new or additional tooling; provided that, prior to incurring any such cost or expense, 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  provides 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: with an estimate of the cost of any such tooling and obtains the prior written approval of 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: for the acquisition thereof.  If 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: fails to approve the acquisition of such new tooling, 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  may, but shall not be required to, satisfy the increased demand.  
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: agrees to purchase at least 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>
Entry: percent (
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry: %) of the amount of its forecasted orders for the immediately succeeding quarterly forecasted period.

Entry: %) of its total requirement for such Product during any of three immediately preceding quarters, 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall be given, if needed, 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  months lead time for the acquisition of new or additional tooling, as the case may be, to satisfy the increased demand.  
Entry: Seller
Entry:  may charge 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: for the cost and expenses of such new or additional tooling; provided that, prior to incurring any such cost or expense, 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  provides 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: with an estimate of the cost of any such tooling and obtains the prior written approval of 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: for the acquisition thereof.  If 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: fails to approve the acquisition of such new tooling, 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  may, but shall not be required to, satisfy the increased demand.

Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>
Entry: percent (

Entry: %) of the amount of its forecasted orders for the immediately succeeding quarterly forecasted period.

Child 45:
Entry: 3.1     
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: represents, warrants and agrees that the Specifications for the Products satisfy 
Entry: Buyer’s 
Entry: requirements for its intended use of the Products.  If at any time during the term of this Agreement, 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: desires to modify the Specifications, 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: shall have the right upon 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>
Entry: days prior written notice to 
Entry: Seller
Entry: , to modify or change the Specifications, subject to 
Entry: Seller
Entry: ’s approval, which approval shall not be unreasonably withheld. Within 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>
Entry: days of receipt by 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  of such notice, 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall notify 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: whether or not it can manufacture the Products according to the modified Specifications, and if so, whether or not 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  would need (
Entry: i
Entry: ) to adjust the price of the Product to reflect any changes in the cost of raw materials, direct 
Entry: labour
Entry:  and overhead that will result from such modification or change, and (ii) to the extent necessary, extend the Delivery Dates for the Products.  If 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  cannot manufacture the Products according to the modified Specifications, or if 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  requests a price increase in excess of 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry: % and the 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: does not accept the adjusted Product price, or the 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: does not accept the extension of the Delivery Dates, 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: may terminate this Agreement.  Neither party shall have any liability arising from such termination, except that 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: shall purchase all Products made for 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: that are in 
Entry: Seller
Entry: ’s inventory and reimburse 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  for the cost of all raw materials and components specific to the Company’s Products purchased on behalf of 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: pursuant to an outstanding purchase order, as of the date that 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  received the Company’s written notice to modify the Specifications.

Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>

Entry: <u>Appendix D</u>

Entry: <u>Design Services</u>
Entry: ”).   Each party shall continue to own all patents, trademarks, copyrights, trade secrets and other intellectual property (
Entry: i
Entry: ) it owned prior to the start of the Design Services (“Existing IP”) and/or (ii) developed outside the provision of the Design Services (“Other IP”).  All modifications, improvements or inventions directly related to the Product which are conceived, reduced to practice, or developed jointly by the parties in the course of the performance of the Design Services shall be owned by 
Entry: Buyer
Entry: , except to the extent such modifications, improvements or inventions constitute 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  Proprietary Information.  “
Entry: Seller
Entry:  Proprietary Information” means 
Entry: Seller
Entry: ’s Existing IP, Other IP and all methods, processes, procedures, knowhow, trade secrets and intellectual property related to the manufacture of the Products.

Child 52:
Entry: 3.4           
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: acknowledges that 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  will be utilizing certain critical suppliers of raw materials and components.  In the event that any supply agreement with a critical supplier is terminated for any reason outside of 
Entry: Seller
Entry: ’s control, or if such critical supplier is unable for any reason outside of 
Entry: Seller
Entry: ’s control to supply 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  with the raw materials or components in the quantities it requires to manufacture the Products for Company, 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall provide 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: with written notice thereof, and 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall utilize reasonable commercial efforts to obtain an alternative supplier with similar pricing and delivery capabilities from its list of approved vendors.  If 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  is unable to obtain an alternative supplier with similar pricing, it shall provide 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: written notice thereof, including the new prices for the Products; provided that if such increase in Product prices is greater than 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry: % during any Contract Year, 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: may terminate this Agreement without liability to either party.

Entry: Seller

Entry: Buyer

Child 64:
Entry: All shipments of Products shall be made F.O.B. 
Entry: Seller
Entry: ’s manufacturing facility.  
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall make commercially reasonable efforts to meet the Delivery Dates requested by 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: in accordance with

Child 68:
Entry: 6.1    
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: shall have 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  
Entry: days from the Receipt Date to inspect the Product.  If 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: determines during its inspection of the Product that the Product does not meet the requirements of the applicable Specifications, 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: shall notify 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  of such nonconforming Product and provide 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  with samples thereof within such 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  day period.  
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall inspect such nonconforming Product within 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  days following receipt of such notice and samples, and within such period provide 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: with the results of its inspection.  If 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  determines that the Product is deficient, 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall, at its expense at its option, either cure such rejection or replace the rejected Product with Product that meets the Specifications.  Any Product that is not inspected or rejected by 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: within the 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  day period shall be deemed to have been accepted by Company.  The 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: and 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall negotiate any disputes in good faith.
Entry:

Child 68:
Entry: 6.1    
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: shall have 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  
Entry: days from the Receipt Date to inspect the Product.  If 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: determines during its inspection of the Product that the Product does not meet the requirements of the applicable Specifications, 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: shall notify 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  of such nonconforming Product and provide 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  with samples thereof within such 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  day period.  
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall inspect such nonconforming Product within 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  days following receipt of such notice and samples, and within such period provide 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: with the results of its inspection.  If 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  determines that the Product is deficient, 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall, at its expense at its option, either cure such rejection or replace the rejected Product with Product that meets the Specifications.  Any Product that is not inspected or rejected by 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: within the 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●]</span>
Entry:  day period shall be deemed to have been accepted by Company.  The 
Entry: Buyer 
Entry: and 
Entry: Seller
Entry:  shall negotiate any disputes in good faith.

Child 93:

Entry: 0
Entry: .1   
Entry: <u>Confidentiality</u>
Entry: . Each party agrees to hold in confidence and refrain from using, distributing, disseminating or disclosing to others any information of the other party that is designated by the discloser as “confidential” or from making or causing to be made, or selling or distributing, any product embodying confidential information, other than pursuant to this Agreement. The restrictions set forth in the preceding sentence shall not apply to information that a receiving party proves: (a)  was, at the time of disclosure hereunder, in the public domain through no fault of the recipient; (b)  was in the possession of recipient prior to disclosure hereunder, as evidenced by recipient's written or tangible evidence; (c)  was disclosed to recipient by a third party that has an independent right to disclose the information; (d)  was independently developed by recipient as evidenced by competent proof; or (e) was required to be disclosed by judicial order, statute or governmental regulation,  provided that the disclosing party is given reasonable prior written notice of any such required disclosure and only to the extent required by such judicial order, statute or governmental regulation.  This Section shall survive termination of this Agreement and any extension thereof, for a period of 
Entry: <span style="color:#000000">[●] </span>
Entry: years.

The restrictions set forth in the preceding sentence shall not apply to information that a receiving party proves: (a)  was, at the time of disclosure hereunder, in the public domain through no fault of the recipient; (b)  was in the possession of recipient prior to disclosure hereunder, as evidenced by recipient's written or tangible evidence; (c)  was disclosed to recipient by a third party that has an independent right to disclose the information; (d)  was independently developed by recipient as evidenced by competent proof; or (e) was required to be disclosed by judicial order, statute or governmental regulation,  provided that the disclosing party is given reasonable prior written notice of any such required disclosure and only to the extent required by such judicial order, statute or governmental regulation.  This Section shall survive termination of this Agreement and any extension thereof, for a period of
